Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon Jo

1)
Only Love is the Greatest Will
The fundamental reason we are born is not in life itself. Even if a father possesses life force alone, without a mother, that life has no relation to me. It is love centered on both the mother and father that connects us. Therefore, love is further than life itself.
The most precious thing is love
The fundamental power of the universe is generated through the same form of reciprocal love relationships in the material world. Thus, no being can exist in this universe without a relationship between subject and object.
Because the most precious thing is love, when love becomes the center, one cannot give or receive it freely, leading to the greatest sadness and pity.
Why did God create the universe? It is a natural conclusion that He created the universe because love was needed. Therefore, humans are born in love, live in love, and return to love.
Where does the greatest love come from? It comes from the complete oneness of subject and object. When they become eternally one, unbreakable by any force, the greatest love will emerge. Through love, unity occurs, through love, life is connected, and through love, ideals are realized.
By becoming one rather than two, something greater emerges; when two lives become one, a greater life is born, and when the ideals of two become one, a greater ideal is realized.
We are born as participants in the place where the lives and ideals of our mother and father are united centered on love. We must understand that we are participants in the place where our parents' love is united, where their lives are connected, and where their ideals are aligned.
Realization of the Ideal of Love
So, where should the realization of the ideal of love begin? From our Unification Church? From the nation? From the world? No matter how much one unifies the world, a person who cannot unify their own family is an unhappy person. The realization of the ideal of love must begin in the family. The family is the cradle of happiness. Therefore, heaven begins in the family. When Jesus, who came to establish heaven on this earth, said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride," it was a statement centered on the family.
Who is in the family? First, there are parents, second, children, third, couples, and then siblings. So, what binds the family together? It is love. Therefore, how can we make the family one? We can make it one through love.
Because love is unchanging, the love of grandparents can become one, the love of parents can become one, and the love of couples can become one. Because love has unifying properties, it can become one. Moreover, because love is intertwined with the motivation of human life, the lives of grandparents can be connected. And ideals can be connected here.
Grandparents pass on to parents. In other words, they pass on to children. The children of grandparents are parents, and the children of parents are us. The place centered on such love is heaven. If any of this is denied, heaven cannot be established.
God is the subject of love and is the one who can integrate the past, present, and future, so loving one's parents means one must also love one's grandparents.
The Path of True Love
Men symbolize heaven, and women symbolize earth. Men dislike being interfered with because they are the subject. Women prefer to be loved rather than to love. Because men symbolize heaven and women symbolize earth, the oneness of man and woman is the oneness of the universe.
Only through love can the universe be governed, and only through love can one become the subject of the universe, so one must think of their partner as greater than the universe. The unchanging love is what connects the two worlds of heaven and earth. Those who live a life woven with love on this earth will go to heaven. The world centered on love is the spiritual world.
When God and each individual human become completely one, men and women will automatically become one, and when perfect couples arise, heaven and earth will be unified.
Where does God want to be? Love arises between a man and a woman, so He wants to be where true men and true women love each other. Because God is present, that love can be eternal, that love can achieve eternal unity, that love can possess eternal life, and that love can embody eternal ideals. Therefore, those who seek (grasp) that love can conquer everything.
Being born in love, growing up in love, and then connecting to another dimension of love means seeking the love of a partner apart from parental love. Parental love can be called reproductive love, and the love of couples can be called mature love. No matter how much couples love each other, without children, they cannot see the completion of love. That is why they desire children. This is the love of completion. Therefore, the process of passing through parental love, couple love, and children's love is the foundation of life and the fundamental path of God's creative love.
The purpose of a family formed centered on true love is not just for the family itself but to establish heaven. It expands from the family to the nation, world, and cosmos centered on a standard that aligns with the purpose of unifying the universe. Thus, one must go to the world and then return.
To save this world, God has sacrificed His most beloved servants and His most beloved sons and daughters, and has allowed many believers to be killed and sacrificed throughout history. Many Christians have been massacred, right? Without striking the fallen world or the enemy, God has forgiven those He loves by striking them.
If one stands in a position to sacrifice their own nation, family, and everything for the world, they can become a saint because they resemble God. God is the center of the greatest holy being, which is why we can call them a holy person.
The path of true love is to advance toward a greater world, even at the cost of one's own side. When viewed from the perspective of our family, when the family exists for society, leaving the family does not mean abandoning it; rather, it means being able to unite with society from that position. When a son grows up, meets a partner, and forms a couple, they may separate from their parents, but through the union of couples, the bond of love with parents can deepen, and by having children, it can grow even larger. When that family goes out into society, it can grow even more. The more it develops, the larger it can become.
If a single person can become a saint in this world, sacrificing their family, tribe, nation, and everything for God and unifying centered on God, then the logic holds that they can participate in the world and the universe that they had previously sacrificed.
One must be able to sacrifice their family for God's will, be able to sacrifice their nation for God's will, and be able to sacrifice this world for God's will. Even so, one must be able to save this cosmos. When something greater is resurrected and victorious, the whole will live.
The Path the Unification Church Must Take
Why does the Unification Church suffer persecution, and why does the teacher remain silent without repaying the enemy? It is because, throughout the long historical process, even after suffering so much death, our Lord, God, remains silent. Then why does God remain silent? It is to save even one more person. That is why the Unification Church is walking this path.
If one treats the enemy as an enemy, they cannot walk the path of love. When a unified world is achieved, there will be no one to complain about them in the past, present, or future. Therefore, living centered on oneself is the path of Satan, while living for others is the path of heaven. This is the shortcut to finding the purpose of love and establishing the ideal world of love.
Our Unification Church members should not only cling to their families after receiving blessings but should also walk the path of sacrifice for the nation or the world. The teacher is the same. Even if it means sacrificing mothers and children, it is for the world. If I were to abandon them in order to find the world and die without achieving my purpose, then abandoning them was for the sake of finding the world, so if God exists on the day I find the world again, He must also restore my family. He must restore my family to be God...
If God were to ask you what your wish is, you would say that your wish is to restore your family and your nation after finding the whole world. Therefore, when this world is restored, the family and the nation will automatically be saved. Those who were sacrificed will automatically participate in the place of glory when that day comes.
That is why you must have hope that even if the nation opposes you and your parents oppose you, you will meet again, and you must endure a little longer. You must walk the path of persecution and misunderstanding with hope.
Thus, the teacher has abandoned his hometown, his nation, and all the Korean churches, suffering persecution and being slandered while fleeing until now. However, he believes that when they surrender, they will surrender one hundred percent, and he endures for that day. We are developing while being chased and pursued.
We are not people of despair but people of hope. How strong are we? Because we are united by an absolute love that cannot be severed by anything, there is no one who can conquer us.
You must understand that only love can bring all victories. You must know that where there is love, eternal victory and eternal heaven are established. Everything is liberated in front of love. The teacher is striving toward that place. *
2)
We Are the Historical Fruit
<Prayer> Beloved Father! Please remember the children gathered here this morning and remember your children scattered across the nation.
Today is particularly the first day of September, welcoming a new month after passing through August. This morning, I earnestly hope and desire that Your mercy, glory, and love may always be with the children who are concerned about Your will.
I understand that this year, 1971, is a significant year centered on Your will. Up to now, two-thirds of this year has passed, and during these eight months, You have accomplished many things together with Your young children. Now, in the remaining one-third of this year, as we follow Your will, I earnestly hope and desire that You will always be with us in Your grace and guide us with increased blessings.
As the children scattered across the nation look up to Seoul this morning, and as the children scattered across the world look up to the Republic of Korea, countless spirits in the spiritual world and millions of saints look down upon this land, we deeply long for Your love to remain upon us from heaven to the world, to the nation, to our church, and to ourselves. We realize that if we do not receive Your love, and if our families, our nation, and this world do not fall under Your love, we will become indebted, and this nation and this world cannot stand before Your will.
As we think about this fact, we must first stand within Your love.
To stand within Your love, we know that we must endure to the end while looking at the path of Your labor and participate in it, so we have come this far, overcoming difficult circumstances in our church path.
As we have gone through difficult processes, we have sworn to You, become aware of You, and made resolutions regarding You at each moment. When recalling all of these, we must advance, and whenever we encounter difficult problems, we must become sons and daughters who can take responsibility even more willingly. Without becoming such sons and daughters, we know well that we cannot fulfill this tremendous task of restoration in our lifetime or through this nation.
If there is one person who represents the providential will of that era, that person is not just one person but represents history, represents the era, and furthermore represents the future and eternity. Therefore, if that one person cannot take responsibility, it does not just end with their inability to take responsibility for their own lifetime but leaves a blemish in history for not having fulfilled their responsibility. Even if that person seems insignificant, they must lead a life distinguished before You because that one person stands in the position of a sacrificial offering for all lives, and we must always be in a position to be dedicated before You.
The fact that we are gathered here today and have formed this connection to serve You is not due to any merit of our own but because of the foundation of goodness that has been passed down from good ancestors through the generations.
comes. It is because there is a will of the Father to unify that relationship and connection through us along with our Father. Therefore, although we meet in one era, he represents the entire historical era, and although he is a single insufficient person, he represents the historical ancestors. Thus, whether we can bear the responsibility of being called and established before the Father today is not merely a matter of our own lives, nor just a matter of our own selves or our families, but rather a matter that encompasses the entire surrounding context, and we must always be aware of this fact.

Moreover, as those who know the principle, we must understand that we cannot bypass the connections of the three eras. Therefore, through the past, present, and future, centered on your will, your desires, and your heart, we must always be nurtured within your protection and grace. We must become sons and daughters who are certain of this.

Please also be with the children who long for this place but cannot attend.

We will surely go. We will surely act, so Father, please do not regard our insufficiencies as lacking. The more we realize our insufficiencies, the more we recognize our shortcomings before you, and we can endure any path of suffering, any difficult situation, and even if we find ourselves at the end of our lives, we can go forth with a heart of gratitude. We believe and know that we will surely occupy a place of results that can be unified with the saying that Heaven makes the wise and knowledgeable feel ashamed through the insufficient ones. Therefore, we earnestly hope and desire that you will always be with us.

We are always aware of how great the effort of the Father is to lead us to a perfect world, yet we find ourselves in a position of indebtedness. Because we are in a position of indebtedness, we should not stand in a high place but rather repay from a low position. If we cannot repay our debts, we must have the heart to offer our own lives as a sacrifice to make amends. We always know that God will never depart from those who have such a heart, so we earnestly hope and desire that you will guide and lead us.

Today is the first day of September, and we dedicate this month to you, Father. We earnestly hope that you will take charge of the remaining one-third of this year. We desire that our lives be woven together with your will, and we hope that this remaining one-third of the year will be protected within your glorious will, and that you will always pave the way for victory.

Please allow us to always have the heart of a child who knows nothing, longing for you. May our hearts be filled with the desire to see you, to yearn for you, and to meet you and live together forever. We hope that our lives will not stray from the path of looking up to Heaven, looking down to the earth, and looking out to the world, shedding tears and living a life of gratitude.

Even if we live difficult lives in this world, we have come to know that the place where Heaven is with us is not a lonely place nor a pitiful one, so please guide and lead us. We earnestly ask and desire that you protect, guide, and lead us on the path we take.

We earnestly hope that you will take charge of this month. Moreover, please bless the children scattered overseas, and as family members and young children from abroad gather in one place for training, please be with them as well. Remember the young daughters on the front lines and the son who is currently in a difficult situation, Father, and take charge of everything.

All authority is before you, so please take charge and lead us according to your pleasing will. I ask again that you handle everything in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We members of the Unification Church are well aware that we bear a historical mission. Sometimes when we pray, we say, "We are a historical fruit."

As you know, the year 1971 is different from previous years. Our church has held many events so far, such as inviting professors for Unification Principle seminars or holding principle public hearings for pastors. Furthermore, we are currently planning and conducting comprehensive training centered around the long-standing members among those in Japan. We have come this far through these busy days.

1971 is a year of historical fruition.

While our intentions are busy, we can see that the situation in our Republic of Korea and the international circumstances are at an increasingly urgent point when viewed from our perspective. We can also glimpse that the flow of all history is moving toward a single fruition. No matter how complicated the situation may be, it is an undeniable fact that through that complicated situation, some providential result will be achieved.

This is also true for our church, which represents the will of providence. No matter how difficult and convoluted the path we have walked has been, we can see that through that process, we are ultimately heading toward a time of fruition that the will desires, or toward such a place.

When viewed this way, the year 1971 is indeed a significant year for achieving fruition more than any other year. Moreover, September, as you know, is the month of fruition. When considering whether the fruition will be successful or not, it is essential that the foundation for fruition is good. Even if the foundation is excellent, the seed planted on that foundation must start as a perfect seed. The seed must be protected by the owner and must be in an environment conducive to growth for a certain period before it can finally bear fruit. The will of providence is the same. Once the will of Heaven has begun, it will surely bear fruit, regardless of the difficulties encountered.

Even when we look at our cultural life today or the historical cultural world, it is the same. The modern civilization we see today can be considered a temperate civilization, which is not a civilization like the fragrant spring season. It is not a civilization that develops progressively toward summer, but rather a civilization that reaches saturation and begins to decline, akin to the autumn season.

Generally, ancient civilizations belonged to the tropical civilization sphere, but now we are in the temperate zone. As this age has become like an autumn civilization, we are threatened by the Soviet communist world, which is akin to the winter season. When we look at this entire history, we can see that the current time symbolizes the autumn season.

To achieve complete fruition, 

In such a time, to become a fruitful living entity, one must possess the vitality to overcome difficult challenges throughout the year. No matter how much rain falls and how much the monsoon comes in summer, one cannot be pushed away by such environmental conditions. One must overcome them. Even when it becomes autumn, one must overcome various difficult conditions until fruition occurs. Only after overcoming those challenges can one be harvested as a true fruit.

Today, the historical providence and all civilizations in the world are the same. When centered around spring, summer, autumn, and winter, the fruition must be able to surpass the winter season. Only then can it greet the new spring season and start anew. 

Similarly, the trends of civilization must not be overwhelmed by the difficulties of the environment during the transitions from summer to autumn and winter. One must surpass these challenges. Only by possessing a new providential civilization that can overcome winter and welcome spring can humanity form a new hope akin to the spring season.

September is the time when everything bears fruit. However, when we focus on the fruition itself, we can understand the environment that has been traversed until now. Whether one has met a good owner, whether the planted land was fertile, or whether the seed was perfect, these facts will manifest in the fruit that appears in autumn after going through the process. Our church is no different. No matter how much the church has gone through the path of suffering, it is undeniable that we are heading toward a time when we can bear fruit.

In this light, we must ask ourselves whether we are walking the path of faith that can achieve perfect fruition, just as we welcome the autumn days in September. This is the most important question.

To do this, we must have well-prepared environmental conditions, and we must have all internal and external contents well-prepared so that we are not overwhelmed by the environment or pushed out by external factors. We must possess the autonomy to overcome these challenges. Only then can we be harvested as a new fruit and remain as seeds of hope for the future. As we reflect on this September, we must think about the value of fruition and ensure that we ourselves can reveal that value.

Moreover, you are well aware that the year 1971 is different from previous years. As mentioned at the beginning of the year, although this year is short, it is a time of historical transition. Furthermore, August was a time of crossing the saturation point. From now until April and May of next year, and even until August, it will be a crucial period. When we see this, we recognize that 1972 will be a time when we must achieve decisive resolutions centered around our intentions. This is not coincidental. That is why the variables in the current world situation are all concentrated in Asia.

What will happen in autumn? The connections that have been made until now, or even if the land is fertile, will begin to separate from that land. Even the best-grown trees will start to shed their leaves. The supply of sap will also begin to cease. Similarly, after going through a saturation state, it will not continue as it is but will transition. When the time comes to surpass that, it will be entering autumn.

In the same way, when we view our intentions, the years 1971 and 1972 are times of crossing a turning point. Therefore, the years 1970, 1971, and 1972 are times when blessed families in our church are mobilized. That is why you know that the women are at the forefront.

Looking at the restoration providence, we see that women must first pioneer individually, then women representing families must go to the front lines to fight against Satan, and afterward, women representing nations must take the lead in the battle. 

Going through such a process means that families must also be separated once. Just as everything separates in autumn, as the time approaches, it will not be that everything comes together and operates as a whole, but rather it will transition through a form of separation into the autumn season.

Looking at the current world situation, the global situation is colliding around Asia. Look! The Soviet Union, China, and North Korea have followed a single line until now, but with China's current actions, North Korea and China are separating. Furthermore, China and the Soviet Union are also separating. Additionally, when we look at the representative nations of the democratic world, such as the United States, Japan, and South Korea, Japan's current movements are causing a separation from the United States. The United States is also acting in a way that seems inseparable from its previous relationships but is separating. As this separation occurs, what will happen? Everything is caught up in a situation of separation.

In such a time of separation, we must not be led by the environment or circumstances that are separating but must secure ourselves completely to inherit a foundation of hope for the future, a fruition that can be providentially established. That entity, whether it be a nation or an organization, must remain as a complete fruit even in the face of a winter that is prone to separation. It must possess the motivation for a new beginning, capable of being planted as a new seed in spring. Without having such content, it cannot be harvested as a complete product before Heaven.

From this perspective, even though our Unification Church may seem to be separating, we are not declining or being consumed from an internal standpoint. Instead, we must stand in a position where we can strengthen and consolidate our vitality, absorbing it as a motivation. Only then can we become true seeds that can welcome spring.

As we welcome this autumn, we must reflect once again on the providential path. For our church, we are transitioning from 1970 to 1971 and then to 1972. When we look at the peaks, these three points are connected. From that perspective, the year 1971 is the most important year.

Therefore, our church will not end as a church itself; we see that various national issues, societal issues, and major political issues are approaching us. We can glimpse that we are at a point where the nation and our church must pledge for a new fruition.

The more we look at this environment, the more we see that as our church stands in such a position, or as the world stands in such a position, the issue lies with you. You must possess the essence of life that has welcomed the autumn season so that no matter how much separation occurs in the environment or how difficult the circumstances may be, all those difficulties do not destroy you but become the motivation and environment for you to complete your own fruition. Knowing this, I hope you will engage in meaningful faith life along with the autumn season. 

3) Realization of Ideals
The realization of ideals means that everything I desire goes well as I wish. Even if what I desire is eternal rather than temporary, it must surely align well.

Realization of God's and Humanity's Ideals
If God exists, then He must have ideals as well. What is the realization of God's ideals? The realization of God's ideals is also that what He desires aligns well.

What does God desire? When we say "desire," the object of desire does not refer to oneself. When I say I desire something, it is based on a relative standard. Is that not so? When we say "my wish," it does not refer to wishing for oneself. It is centered around what has already been achieved.
It is not about wishing for something, but wishing for something that has not been realized yet. It is relative, you see. When we ask what a wish is, a person increasingly desires better things, and eventually, it becomes an ideal. Therefore, the most important issue is how to realize what I desire.

September 1, 1971 (Wednesday), Cheongpyeong Training Center.  
* This statement was made at the 2nd National Church Leaders' Retreat.

So when you, as church leaders, pray and go out to act, what is your wish? For church leaders, the wish is likely to evangelize many people. Therefore, the important question is how to realize that ideal as a church leader. 

Then, what path should church leaders take? They must follow the path of restoration. They must follow the path of restoration, but whose path is that? It is not my path. It is the path that God walks, which is not my own. Isn't that right? 

What does it mean to realize the ‘ideal’? The ‘ideal’ refers to the ‘creation ideal,’ but what is that creation ideal? The highest ideal for us as humans is to meet God, right? Then what is God's ideal? Wouldn't God's ideal also be to meet Himself? God's ideal is to meet a perfect partner. For God, the perfect partner is not Himself but humanity. Therefore, God's ideal is in humanity, and humanity's ideal is in God. The place where these ideals meet is where the creation ideal is realized. Isn't that so? 

What God desires is humanity, and what humanity desires is God. When does that ideal get realized? It cannot be realized by looking from just one side. If God desires but humanity does not, what is that? And if humanity desires but God does not, what is that? Both must look towards each other and meet. When they meet, what happens? They come to like each other. Liking each other is the realization of the ideal.

So God wants to meet humanity, and humanity wants to meet God, but where and how should they meet? That is the problem. Where should they meet? “They meet in the heart.” They meet starting from our hearts. Of course, there are many other places, but they meet from our hearts. For that to happen, the heart and body must like each other. The heart and body must like each other, but they have not liked each other, which is why the ideal has not been realized. To realize the ideal, the heart and body must like each other. So did the heart and body like each other? Not liking each other is a conflicting factor. This is the problem. The heart likes one thing, but the body dislikes it, and the body likes one thing, but the heart dislikes it, leading to a position that contradicts the standard that God and humanity desire.

Fixing this is religion. Religion has emerged to try to realize the ideal again. It seeks to realize the ideal through religion. If it is done, results will come out of it. Making that happen is the consciousness of religion. It is about removing one thing to create harmony. When the body and heart are harmonized and become one, a revolution occurs in the body. (Due to poor recording conditions, some portions could not be organized.)

The ideal is realized from the unity of the body and heart. 

Humans have a conflict between the heart and body. The heart and body are at odds with each other. They are in opposing positions. The heart and body should be united and form a straight line, but instead, they are in conflict, leading to discord. Therefore, we must make this into a straight line. For that, we must unite centered on God. We must shift to become straight, and if we cannot shift, we must cut off that part. That is why it is a serious problem. Isn't that so? We must cut off the place of sin as much as we have grafted. We must deny as much as we have grafted.

That is why until now, religion has come out by denying. Denying what? Denying the body. What happens when you deny? What occurs when you deny? It becomes positive. Because there is an essential element that allows the body and heart to harmonize according to God's creation law, if a certain amount of sacrifice is made, they will automatically harmonize. If you deny for just three years, unity will occur. So, it is said to deny. It is to deny the body.

The most important question is where to start realizing the ideal. Where should we start? “From the heart and body.” When the heart and body are united, that is, when the subject and object as mentioned in the principle completely reciprocate, God will be present there. Why does God dwell there? Would God dwell there for the heart and body to fight? No. He dwells there to create goodness. Why is it good? Because it is a position of reciprocity.

For human bodies to reciprocate horizontally, they must first reciprocate vertically. Why must they reciprocate vertically? Because that is the principle of heaven and earth. Movement begins from there. When there is complete reciprocity, God will definitely stand in a proportional subjective position. Humans are meant to reciprocate centered on the vertical. When that happens, it does not just end with reciprocity. Action will definitely occur. It means that sons and daughters will come forth. It means that the act of reproduction can occur.

When the positive and negative of electricity act, a reaction and an opposite pole are bound to arise. Isn't that so? When the opposite pole arises, the action of three-dimensional poles automatically occurs. Therefore, when a couple unites, children are born. Because the universe is fundamentally structured that way, when a couple unites, the reaction and opposite pole of that person appear, leading to the birth of children. (Due to poor recording conditions, about 25 minutes of speech could not be organized.)

Are you the subject of realizing the ideal? 

The word ideal itself is relative. Isn't that so? When we say, “I think ideally,” isn’t that an ideal? It is thinking splendidly. But is it splendid thinking to say, “Ah, the food was really delicious” after eating? That is all past thought. (Laughter) Isn’t that so? Splendid thinking is thinking about the other, and that is the most splendid thought.

Then, we must realize the ideal, but the important question is how to do it concretely. The world now is an evil world. Therefore, the question is whether you can become the subject who can realize the ideal here or not. The subject is you, the church leaders, and whether you can realize the ideal or not is the issue. What is happening in the current satanic world is all conflict. Isn’t that so? “Yes.”

Only the love of the family can make the realization of the ideal possible. 

Can the ideal be realized through any means and methods? “No.” Then what can make it happen? “Principle-based…” What principle-based thing can make it happen? Only with the love of the family can the ideal be realized. This is the law of heaven. Do you understand? “Yes.” It is the love of the family. For that to happen, the divided family must be restored before God’s will, and for that, women must be restored. Without the love of the family, the realization of the ideal cannot happen.

What is the purpose of God’s providence of salvation in dealing with the world until now? It is to realize the ideal. Then what must be brought forth? Should it be with authority? Think about it. What must be brought forth? “Love.” It must be brought forth with love. What kind of love must be brought forth? “The love of the family.” It is the love of the family, but which love must be brought forth first? The love of the couple? “The love of the parents.” If we must bring forth the love of the parents, there must be children who can receive that love. But if there are no children to receive the love of the parents, can that love come forth? (Laughter) Answer me. The love of the parents is good, but to bring forth the love of the parents, there must be children who can receive that love. Therefore, we set the other as a hope and learn to love that child. This is the providence of restoration. This is how we practice the love of the family.

If God were to come forth with the love of the parents, He could not face God with fallen love. Can He? It was because the fight against injustice was so fierce, and we were in such a serious state of emergency that once we went to the front lines, we could not return to the rear. We understand that we were in a position where we could not return once we went out due to the battle. We sincerely thank You for bestowing Your love upon us, who have become weary with time.

You did not call us for our own sake. If I make a mistake, it would be good if only I would perish, but when we consider our responsibilities, we know that if I make a mistake, it affects the village, the township, and the county. Whenever we look back at the history of the Unification Church, we cannot help but feel how fearful those who have taken responsibility are. Before heaven and before the history of the Unification Church, we must become the vanguard of the restoration providence, promising that we will leave behind a good standard and never leave behind an evil standard, even if we cannot be of help.

In the time of the Fall, it was a place that could not be forgiven, but now, at this time, we must struggle and declare that we will never stand in a place that cannot be forgiven again, even if it means death, and we must become Your sons and daughters who strive day and night to fulfill our responsibilities. We earnestly wish and hope that we may become Your sons who endure until the end, realizing that You are looking for content through them.

Father, please protect the churches across the nation. As they return this time, may they establish a new foundation and fulfill the wishes of the nation until they can stand before Your will. May I become a holy son who is buried in the earth and becomes fertilizer to bloom the buds of the nation, realizing that there is nothing more to wish for than that. I earnestly hope and wish that wherever they return, new heavenly connections will be formed, and through them, may the history of heaven be awakened.

I have come to understand that ideal realization cannot happen without Your love, Father. May we become a holy group that fulfills the responsibility of the priesthood to atone for this land with the heart of parents, the heart of couples, and the heart of children.

The sons who are prostrated in this place, it is now time to return. With a great mission before us, we must now part ways and establish new connections. Even if we stand in a position where the past and future are different, our hearts for the Father and for the Father's nation are the same, so as we feel that the wounds are great, we ask once again that we may become holy sons who overcome with our own wounds and remain until the end.

I have offered all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
This morning, we hope that you will fill each of our individual spirits with blessings according to our individual conditions. May this morning be one where all people bow before you, offering their earnest hearts in anticipation of a glorious moment.

We witness that countless people living on this earth do not know whether the Father exists or not. When we think about how many children there are who are indispensable to you, whether in your heart, your circumstances, or your desires, among the standard bearers of those I wish to love among humanity, we feel an exceedingly, exceedingly small number. When we ask who among your children, who are bowed down here, can step forward and answer ‘I’ when asked who is the son or daughter who establishes a connection with your heart and swears to fulfill your requirements, we hope that there will be even a few sons who can do so.

Father, who always labors with this insignificant and weak group, who patiently advises us even in lonely places, who takes full responsibility for the environment of sorrow and steps forward to pave the way for our safety, as we think of you as such a Father, please forgive us, your unfilial children, for not having you as the master of our hearts. Please forgive us, your inadequate children, who did not realize that you are the Father who continues to create history today by resurrecting us infinitely and eternally with life.

Now, as we adjust our collars and look upon your holy image, we are looking forward to a time when we can be filled with admiration and longing. If you have anything you wish to command, please come and allow it to penetrate our bodies and hearts, and if we cannot go toward the place you desire through the new commandment, we earnestly hope and wish that you will strike us with a whip to lead us there.

Now we have entered September. We have faced many hardships in the year 1971. We have held many events. If we have significant responsibilities and missions ahead of us, it is to offer a sacrificial offering that can take on the final judgment seat you must take before this nation and the world. We must become a group that can realize that this responsibility lies with us.

Father, please look upon the current situation of this country with sorrow and remember it. You must take responsibility for the future destiny of the Republic of Korea. No one can lead this nation, and no one can take responsibility for it; only you can align this nation with the direction of heavenly fortune. Please bind our individual hearts and the heart of this nation together so that this nation can align itself with your desired will. We earnestly hope and wish for you to work in this way.

No matter how capable a person may be, no one can block heavenly fortune, and we must comply with the laws of heavenly fortune. Every time we think about this, we realize that your heart must be within the hearts of many who are leading this nation, and before the final decisive situation, we ask you to present the point that must inevitably lead to the fulfillment of your providential will.

Our church wishes to walk the path desired by the whole world, and you know well that we have been struggling and fighting to pledge for the victory of that one day desired by heaven and earth. Even if there is sorrow today, we do not look forward to standing in a sorrowful position for our personal circumstances at this moment. When we feel that it is the pride of children with unification thought to want to share in the sorrow along with the fate of the nation and the world for the hope of tomorrow, we earnestly hope and wish that this place where we have bowed down before you may be a place that can connect the victory of heaven beyond the nation to the world and the cosmic relationship.

Let this time be one that removes each person's selfish desires and allows us to inherit the true heart of heaven. We earnestly hope and wish that this may become the substance of victory that can pledge for the day of victory you command.

We are to be offered as sacrifices before you, yet we are unable to do so. We earnestly hope that you will lead us to the altar of sacrifice, whether by force or by drawing us.

When Abraham, taking his ignorant son Isaac to Mount Moriah, was asked by Isaac where the lamb for the sacrifice was, and he replied, ‘That is not for you to worry about,’ we feel how much sorrow must precede your heart as we consider the hearts of such parents.

When we think about how often we have worried about ourselves and our surroundings before worrying about your heart, we must now become a time when we first worry about your heart and maintain your flow, becoming sons and daughters indispensable before you and the people of that nation. This time must not only be a realization but also a time to pledge with conviction. We earnestly hope and wish for you to allow this.

As we lament our unfortunate selves born into an evil world, the more earnest our hearts are looking toward the hopeful kingdom, the more we must realize that we cannot help but worry about when we will determine the point of victory.

In the crossroads of whether to go left or right, we are a pitiful group that cannot choose the path of destiny, and we think about the responsibility that remains for you to guide us here. As we consider that you, who have come through the path of labor, must make us pledge this decisive responsibility at the final crossroads, we cannot help but blame our own inadequacies. However, we are beings who cannot live apart from your embrace, and we cannot live outside of your arms. Therefore, even if we must die, we have the single-minded desire to rush toward that place and stay there. We earnestly hope and wish that you will lead this group to be sufficiently trained to stand on the path of the world you desire and love us.

This morning, we know that many children are offering their devotion while looking toward this place, even if it is lacking. Please be with them, and be with the young daughters who are carrying the mission of the times and the overall responsibility. Whenever they find themselves in tearful and difficult circumstances and call upon heaven, may you personally manifest and please do not stand in a place of ignorance.

Their standing in such a place is because of your will, and it is to fulfill your desire to seek and love this nation. Therefore, please open the way of victory so that they may praise the glory of tomorrow. Although we are lacking today, we earnestly ask that you allow us to become daughters who are trusted by you and a group that is in that environment.

Now, we offer our inadequate hearts and bodies before you. If you have anything you wish to command, please do so through your children. Please apply your desire to discern good and evil from our very selves to the entire environment, and we earnestly hope and wish that you will open the way to connect to the nation and the world.

Father, please be with all those who value this day and praise you. Please quickly grant the path of life to the countless religious people and good-hearted individuals scattered around the world, so that they may be bound together in the form of tomorrow and become indispensable groups in your nation. We earnestly ask for the grace and love of the eternal God to be poured out upon the children gathered here and upon the countless groups. We ask this again and conclude all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We are well aware that the land we live in is not good, and we often feel the desire to pursue our good selves. Many people are aware of their individual positions, and they think about how they will take responsibility for this issue, whether as individuals, societies, nations, or the world. In particular, many members of our Unification Church feel this more acutely from the position of taking responsibility for the whole realm.

However, fallen humanity cannot achieve the purpose of pursuing goodness just by pursuing it and following that path. Because there is God, the subject of goodness, and there is Satan, the subject of evil, we have seen through providence that we cannot find the progressive position of goodness without establishing conditions that both God and Satan can recognize.

In other words, to move toward a better position of goodness from today’s standpoint, we must pay some corresponding price. Without doing so, we cannot reach a better position of goodness. Therefore, we know that the principle that God must present the condition of indemnity corresponding to that or that humans must present it does not change.

To move toward a better position of goodness, one must pay the price. If there are those who have hope today and pledge for tomorrow, the greater that hope is, the more they must become those who advance toward that hope. To become such a position, one must make efforts or pay sacrifices behind the scenes. To pursue something of greater value, one must pay a price that can be commensurate with or proportional to that value, regardless of the environment or history. This has been the historical reality, and we know that it is an inevitable path in our search for a better way in reality.

From this perspective, if God exists, then God must also be on the path he pursues, and he must also pay a price in front of a better purpose. How much more so for us, who live within the realm of evil and fall? No one can escape this official law.

In this regard, when standing on the path of pursuing goodness, one cannot simply attain the joy corresponding to the standard of goodness they are looking at just by having a heart that faces goodness and looks toward it. The greater that joy is, the more one must reach it as a result of having paid the price for it. Without paying that price, one cannot attain the corresponding joy.

In this light, the same principle must apply in the context of God’s providential restoration. God seeks to find better individuals through better paths. Throughout the historical ages, there have been many people, but in each era, God has sought better people. Establishing better people and finding a world of greater value in goodness is the path that history has pursued, and we cannot see it as anything other than the purpose of historical development.

Historical Development Laws
If we look at it this way, the question arises as to who among the many saints and righteous figures that have appeared throughout history was a better person. From the time of Adam, through Abel, Noah, Abraham, Moses, John the Baptist, and up to the time of Jesus, and even to the time of Jesus’ apostles who wove the history of Christianity, it is difficult to say that history has only followed a progressive and developmental path. In some eras, there were those who occupied high positions, while in others, there were downhill paths, and at times, there were correct paths, while at other times, there were times when paths crossed and direction was lost.

The development of history must be better today than yesterday, and tomorrow must be better than today. No one wishes for next year to be worse than this year, nor for the following year to be worse than next year, nor for the future to be worse than the present. However, even if there is someone among the leaders who can inherit the global direction of goodness in that era, it cannot be said that the person who inherits the baton is necessarily better than the previous person.

Therefore, those living today must pursue the way of the saints. They must pursue the way of good people who can represent the world. They seek to determine who is better and who is more valuable.

Although many people have existed until now, when it comes to the question of who is a saint and who is better, no one has pursued responsibility or tried to distinguish that.

There are those who pursue someone as a global representative if they align with their thoughts and direction, and there are those who strive to connect their lives with that representative’s standards. However, no one has made efforts to discern how much value the person they are facing holds in the historical era or on the path of pursuing truth, or to distinguish their position in relation to others.

However, even if such humans do not exist, if God exists, then God can clearly distinguish which people stand on such standards, which are better, and which are worse.

If we are a family or if we have many servants, we will seek out better people among them. If there is someone who is one step ahead of a better person, we will demand that person. Therefore, history has not been continued through lesser or less capable people, but rather through better people. God wishes for history to be passed down in that way.

The People God Chooses for the Development of the Restoration Providence
As we know, Abel in Adam’s family did not fulfill his purpose. So, when it comes to the person who inherits Abel’s purpose, should they be a lesser person or a better person than Abel? Without a doubt, they must be a better person than Abel. Should they only be better in some aspects? No, they must be better in all aspects. Humanity, as well as the higher God, cannot help but desire that one surpasses the flat standards and reaches the three-dimensional standards, that is, to be better in all areas.

Therefore, Noah must surpass Abel in terms of faith. He must also surpass him in terms of service. We should consider it natural that God could not help but seek a person who could surpass Abel in all aspects.

However, if the purpose was not fulfilled centering on Noah, and if God could not find the purpose of goodness and the standard of goodness he sought through Noah, then the next person must inherit that purpose. If there is someone who will inherit that, they cannot be lesser than Noah.
must be better than Noah. When we consider what conditions can present the argument that Abraham is better than Noah, we must ask: will it be a more comfortable position than Noah's, or a more difficult one? In a comfortable position compared to Noah's, one cannot become better than Noah. One must be in a position where all conditions are more challenging than Noah's, hosting God and overcoming difficult environments.

When we look at this, was Abraham in such a position? Did Abraham work harder than Noah in a more difficult situation? If so, in what environment was he better than Noah? Abraham lived as the son of Terah in a free environment, in a living space that was enviable to anyone. Therefore, the one difficult thing for such an Abraham was to break away from the familiar comforts of his parents or hometown, which could serve as a resting place or a cradle of comfort.

However, we know that God demanded such a position. Abraham received God's sudden command to leave Ur of the Chaldeans, his hometown. It is difficult to leave immediately upon receiving the command to depart. If it were a place where one could wait with hope for tomorrow, it might be different, but to leave everything familiar—his hometown, his family—immediately upon receiving the command is undoubtedly a very difficult task.

Leaving was vague. If he had been told, "If you leave, this will happen, and these will be the results," it would have been easier, or if he had been informed that "you will be better off than now," it might have been more manageable. But to leave his beloved hometown without such assurances is a daunting task.

Moreover, it is certain that his parents would have opposed such a departure, so Abraham must have left secretly. He likely left without telling his siblings or relatives. Would he have left in broad daylight when everyone could see? Surely, he would have sought a way out under the cover of night or dawn. In such a situation, where there was no clear purpose or discernible environmental conditions, to leave simply upon receiving a heavenly command is exceedingly difficult.

Noah had the limit of 120 years set before him when he received his command, but Abraham had to deny everything about himself and leave without any such conditions or assurances. This must have been more challenging than for anyone else. In this light, Abraham is someone who overcame the most difficult emotional and psychological challenges.

When we look at Moses, he was in a position of great glory. As the son of Pharaoh's daughter, he had the potential to influence the sovereignty of Egypt in the future, and if he had hopes or ambitions, they could have been greater than anyone else's. He was in a position of happiness, yet he took on what seemed like insignificant tasks centered around the Israelite people, denying all the circumstances around him and having to transcend even the issues of life and death. Moses must have had such thoughts. However, in loving his people, the glory of his own life and the glory of his established environment were not the issues; he was not concerned with being comfortable. He believed that he should not place his people in a position of suffering greater than his own and wanted to elevate the future of the nation and Israel above his own glory. Thus, he set out, disregarding all his own glory and committing himself to the path of suffering and hardship. This is not a simple matter; to leap from the highest position to the lowest is exceedingly difficult.

Yet, Moses did not receive any assurance from God regarding his future. God did not call him and command him to act in this way. His love for his people led him to act in anger, and he found himself in a position where everything he had was rejected for the sake of the Israelite people.

However, during his 40 years in the wilderness of Midian, Moses faced circumstances that would have led him to resent the Israelite people, yet he did not blame them. Instead, he worried about the future of the Israelite nation and blamed the Egyptians, who had become his enemies. He did not resent the Israelite people. When they suffered, he bore that suffering gracefully and maintained a heart willing to walk the path of suffering in the wilderness of Midian, living a life of deep gratitude before God, a life that could not be exchanged for anything else. Moses did not stand in that position because he received a promise from God or a command.

From this perspective, the position of affirming the value of being better is not something that can be found in the progressive environment we know today, even if we encounter it in our daily lives.

Who is the greatest filial son, loyal subject, patriot, or saint? If there is a filial son, who is the true filial son among them? Is it the one who sacrifices his entire life for his parents and shows filial piety until he is 70 or 80 years old, or is it the young person who sacrifices his life for his parents? No matter how long someone has been a filial son, he cannot compare to the one who gave his life in youth. Similarly, a loyal subject is determined after death, after sacrificing his life. A true filial son is also determined in the place where life is at stake, as we have seen many times throughout history.

When seeking the truth, if one seeks it in a good environment, in a well-prepared position, versus someone who sacrifices their life in a less favorable position, who holds more value? It goes without saying. If there is a truth that can be found without effort in a fully prepared environment, how precious could that be? Yet, such a person should be regarded with caution. The truth is not woven together in a smooth environment. There cannot be a truth that remains from a smooth environment.

For the truth to be passed down and remain in the current position through historical processes, it must have gone through severe struggles and overcome unfortunate adversities. The truth must have been found in such positions. If someone inherits such truth and seeks to protect it while searching for it in a joyful position where they can be free and hopeful, I do not see that person as truly qualified to face the truth. However, if someone has faced more tragic historical sorrow, has overcome more suffering, has encountered more difficulties, or has worked hard to find the truth while becoming a slave to unfortunate circumstances, and ultimately has risked their life in the process, then that person becomes truly qualified to face the truth.

Among those who have struggled for the truth throughout history, the one who has suffered the most while pursuing the value of truth will be the rightful heir to that truth. If there is someone who has worked hard for the truth, lived a miserable life for the truth, and stood in a position where they could shed blood for the truth, then it is only natural that they would want to be managed by that person and possess what that person has.

Even if there are many patriots in the Republic of Korea, who among them is the greatest patriot? It is the one who, when the nation is in chaos, does not merely worry about the situation and serve loyally but thinks broadly about the past, present, and future, walking the path of suffering and, if there is no way to overcome it, is willing to sacrifice their life to open that path.

Among those who have made such sacrifices, if three people share the same heart and experience, but two die easily while the other is captured by enemies and suffers a gruesome death—hands torn, eyes gouged, ears cut, nose severed, legs broken—who among the three would join the ranks of the greatest patriots? It goes without saying that it would be the one who suffered the most tragically. This is how I see it.

If this is true for a nation, then among the saints of the world, who would occupy the highest rank? It would be the one who suffered the most tragically in their sacrifice. No one else could occupy the highest position.

In all matters occurring in our society and living environment, the one who sacrifices more and dedicates themselves more sincerely to their purpose becomes the master. This is how I see it.

In this light, what about God? Can we think that God, while human affairs are as they are and historical circumstances are what they are, would be any different? It is the same.

Then, who is the pitiful person? It is the one who lives in a miserable position. The one who lives miserably and loses their life is the truly pitiful person. When we consider this, if there is a true master of this world, what kind of person would that master be? Would it be someone who cautiously observes others, acting only when it benefits them, or someone who, when their own benefit is substantial, is proportionally prepared to sacrifice? Such a person may be a temporary master but cannot be a historical master.

If God exists, does God truly love this world? Is God a master of love? God is undoubtedly the master of love and the subject of love. If God has been the eternal master who has loved this world until now, then He must be the one who works harder than anyone else and holds the qualifications to be in a more miserable position than anyone else. Otherwise, He cannot be a master.

A self-made person does not neglect even the rag lying in their yard, examining it to see if it can still be used. They do not overlook any of their belongings. Why? Because they have a habit of valuing even the smallest item in their past, they will always reassess what they have not discarded. When we see this, it becomes clear that the one who values things is indeed that person.

In this light, if there is a God who is the center of the universe, the center of human history, and the protagonist of love before humanity, what kind of being must that God be? Should He be the one sitting on a comfortable throne of glory, calling out, "Come here!" and expecting a response of "Yes, yes"? Absolutely not. A parent with children, if their child is suffering, takes a position that transcends that child's suffering, willing to sacrifice their own life for the sake of their child, ready to give up their life before their child. This is what determines the absolute position of a parent in a family. No parent would deny being the child's mother or father. This is impossible for the absolute God as well. Why? Because a parent always holds the position to sacrifice their life for their child. One who possesses such a heart can always occupy the position of a master. You all know this well.

When we consider this, if God exists, He must be someone who voluntarily comes to a position more miserable than that of humanity. If such a being exists, He is someone we should be grateful for. If such a being is undoubtedly present in our individual lives, He is the one we should be most grateful to. If such a being exists, when I have something to command, I would want to receive that command from Him; if I have a desire to live, I would want to live with Him; if I want to do something, I would want to do it with Him; and if there is a way to love, I would absolutely want to love with Him. This is something you must acknowledge.

From this perspective, when we trace the path of the providence of restoration, when Adam and Eve fell, did only they go to that position of fall while God stood in a good place, watching and scolding, ready to punish them with a whip of curses? No, that is not the case. As the moment of Adam and Eve's fall approached, if there was anyone who felt more sorrow and pain than they did, it would be God, who is the true master.

When Noah, after 120 years of labor, saw his hopes for fulfilling God's will turn to a crossroads of despair, did God look at Noah, who was grieving, and say, "You must endure this sorrow because I commanded you to do so"? No, that would not be the case. When Noah shed tears of sorrow, the master who commanded him also wept.

Have you thought about Noah's family? Noah built the ark on a mountaintop. If it were on flat ground, it might be understandable, but building an ark on a mountaintop is beyond common sense; it surpasses reason. From a normal perspective, Noah's actions were almost those of a madman. To build a boat, one should do so by the river, yet he built it on a mountain, which defies logic.

Would the God who commanded this have done so lightly? No. God, who knows better than anyone that Noah must walk a path of unbearable hardship, did not command him with an easier path in mind. He must have wanted Noah to endure a path of suffering because there were even more difficult conditions that needed to be resolved. How sorrowful must God's heart have been? It must have been indescribably sorrowful.

Therefore, in the tense moment of whether Noah would accept that command, when Noah chose to comply, was there anyone who rejoiced more than God? And was there anyone who could be more sorrowful than God? It is only in such a position of being able to bear joy and sorrow that one can be in the position of God.

Consider the purpose behind God commanding Noah to build the ark for 120 years. Think about it. Noah had a wife and children. He had a family. Yet he turned his back on that family for 120 years, cutting off his entire life as if he were cutting a cord, engaging in what seemed like madness. What then?
Ladies, think about it from the perspective of your husband if he were to do such things. Also, young men or middle-aged men, consider it from the perspective of having such a father. Would you be able to trust such a husband or father? You would call him a mad father, not just a mad man. What do you think? Think about it.

When Noah went up the mountain to build the ark, would his wife have thought, "It's lunchtime, I need to bring lunch to my husband. Our husband will surely become a beloved son of God..."? Would the sons have thought that way? There’s no way they would have. They would have been constantly complaining. For 120 years, they would have been grumbling. If they had a falling out after a year, would they have been grumbling for 120 years? If they started complaining after about 50 years, they would have complained for 70 years. Isn’t that right?

When the husband hears some nonsense from the sky, or in a daze, and says, "I must stake my life on this," would the wife respond, "Oh, really? I wanted that too, and since you are saying you will do it first, that’s truly wonderful. I will actively support you." Do you think there could be a wife like that? Ladies, think about it. Raise your hand if you think you could do that. Let me ask you one thing. If from the moment they met, their opinions clashed, wouldn’t Noah's wife have been the most unfortunate person in the world for 120 years? And if there were children, wouldn’t they have called their father a madman, saying, "For 120 years... what, to judge the world with water? You should build the ark by the riverside, not on top of a mountain?" 

No one was bringing the materials to him. So, he must have prepared everything by himself and carried it all the way up the mountain to build the ark. This is what you would call a supreme madman among madmen. When you think about it this way, would the sons have welcomed their father? Young gentlemen who believe well in the Unification Church, if you were in such a position, would you have said, "You must go all the way"? 

When looking at this, why did God do that? It was to find the wife of wives, to find the family of families. There are countless men and countless families in the world, but God was looking for a family that He could love entirely. A family that God could love entirely must have the right connections and traditions established.

Considering these issues, if Noah’s wife had said when he overslept, "It’s already six in the morning. Why are you so late today?" then she could have been like a diamond embedded in the crown that Noah wore. Isn’t that right? If the sons had thought that way, when they brought forth the issue of being sons and daughters who could provide satisfaction representing the family in human history, there would be no one to praise except for Noah’s sons.

When viewed this way, the mission given to Noah was not to make his family miserable or to ruin them but to place them in a very honorable position, one that could be the best of all. Wouldn’t it have been the absolute being's wish for them to become a family that even the enemy Satan could not follow, a family that no one from the satanic world could touch? When you think about it this way, the 120 years that God gave to Noah had the purpose of having him build the ark, but behind the scenes, God must have been looking forward to Noah establishing a foundation to become a heavenly base.

We must also consider how sad God must have been looking at Noah. When thinking about these issues, what would have happened when the environment that God desired was broken by Noah’s wife? What would have happened when it was broken by the children? Would the wife have complained to Noah or not? Would the sons and daughters have shown filial piety or not? Raise your hand if you think they did show filial piety. Let me ask you one thing. Since Noah worked a lot, he must have come home in the evening and eaten a lot. So, during that mealtime, he must have been mistreated. If she complained, it would have been during that time. What kind of food would Noah have eaten? If she had prepared food for him, it would have been barley rice. They would have eaten first... But still, would the wife have remained silent when she was complaining? "Why is this like this...?" she would have grumbled. She must have had a straightforward personality. So, do you think she dressed him well? Imagine Noah, walking around in rags in that neighborhood.

Looking at that, would the wife have thought, "That man is still lucky"? Wouldn’t she have thought that? Noah’s sons, being born as children, might not have been able to do anything, but if Noah had a brother, he might have grabbed Noah by the neck and silently expressed his feelings, trying to stop him in every possible way. If there had been parents, they would have stood on the street every day and made a fuss. Think about it. Would that have happened or not?

Such stories are not recorded in the Bible, but looking around your life, you can understand these issues. When thinking about these issues, would God’s heart have been at peace? No. Every time such problems arose, the expectations of the wife were shattered, the expectations of the children were shattered, and the expectations of the family were shattered. God, looking at Noah, who had no choice but to be dragged along and subjected to restrictions, was in a precarious position, wondering if the tremendous covenant He had promised would be broken or not, hoping that at least Noah could carry this through and match it. Wouldn’t Noah have thought about wanting to give up? "Why did I do this?"

But would God have said every time, "Noah, Noah, you must not do that. A few years have passed, so a few years remain." Calculating, "50 years have passed, so now 70 years are left. Can’t you endure that?" Would He have comforted him like that? God cannot lead history while comforting him like that.

Even worldly men say, "A man’s word is worth more than gold," but since Noah made a promise with God, when God said, "Noah, I am the Lord of heaven and earth. After 120 years, I will surely do such and such, so you must prepare the ark. No matter what suffering you face for 120 years, overcome it and build the ark," would Noah have thought about whether he could go on in such an environment after saying, "Yes"? If he didn’t think about that, then that would be a lie.

If Noah usually went out to work at seven o'clock, and if he was supposed to go out at that time but spent time thinking and ended up going out after eight, nine, ten, or even eleven o'clock, let’s say he missed a day. There might have been days he missed. If there was a day he missed, what would God’s heart have been like? Would God have said, "You did well. You are thinking as you should. Good. Keep thinking like that"? Noah missing a day would have felt like a thousand years to God. Wouldn’t it? That one day could have been an unfair day that might have interrupted thousands of holy events. That unfairness of that day could remain as the unfairness of heaven and earth. Would God have been pleased? What do you think? It’s a shocking situation.

Therefore, we need to respect, praise, and commend Noah, but we must also think about how sad, miserable, lonely, and unfair God must have felt looking at Noah. We must recognize that there are not many people today who think about that.

That is why God can punish Noah and bless him, as He has the qualifications to do so. How could He punish Noah if He did not have that? God, who has the absolute authority to punish and to govern life and death, must be someone who thinks more painfully than anyone else about the miserable paths of human life and must be the one who leads the way to recover humanity from that place of suffering, not just a spectator.

Is God just giving blessings? Absolutely not. Blessings do not just roll in. When God gives a blessing to one person, there are thousands and tens of thousands of paths He must navigate to come back and recover before He can give that blessing. The Completion of Sacrifice
A sacrifice is in place of oneself.
What is a sacrifice? It is in place of oneself. Just as you know through the Word, God does not conduct the work of restoration haphazardly. Let me tell you a funny story. When I fled, there were three companions. They are sitting over there now. I carried a guy with a broken leg on a bicycle and brought him out over a thousand miles. As we came down, the national road was filled with retreating soldiers, so we went over the mountain ridges and slopes. There are many anecdotes from that time. The biggest problem we faced while coming out was cooking rice. Since we couldn't carry rice along with our luggage, we had no choice but to steal at that time. (laughter)

"Isn't it a shame that Teacher Moon of the Unification Church is stealing?" you might think, but (laughter) I made them steal. We searched through the abandoned homes. At that time, it was okay to steal. Even if we didn't search, the Chinese army would come and search. When fleeing, you have to go lightly. If I die, it would be a big deal. 

I thought it was okay for me to die, but when I thought about how the heavens and earth would mourn, I realized I shouldn't die, so I thought I had to live. When it was time to cook in the morning, what rice did I have? So I went into a nearby house early in the evening to get rice for breakfast. There was rice in every house. When I brought back rice, I told them to take the first rice they saw. If you start picking and choosing rice, you will really become a thief. Do you understand what I mean? You have to do it this way to avoid being labeled a thief. Also, when heaven and earth see, they might think, "Wow, these guys are taking someone else's rice, but they are still decent people," and at least feel some sympathy.

So I told them to open the rice jar and take whatever they found first, whether it was millet or corn. I said you shouldn't bring back something else after taking that. I told them to take the first thing they saw. So when entering a house, they would look for rice jars, rice jars, rice jars. (laughter) If there was millet, they would bring back millet. If they always brought back the same thing, they would get scolded, so from then on, they would be more careful about what they brought back.

Sometimes when cooking, I could smell that they were cooking with something they had picked up from a graveyard. You can tell just by looking at it. So I said, "What are you cooking with, you guys?" They knew about such things and could talk about it. Because of that, the Unification Church has survived until now. If you were like you are now, we would have already perished. (laughter)

When it came time to eat, we always had plenty, but there was only one pot, so we could only cook one pot's worth. Would it be possible to cook like we were living in a refugee situation? There was only one simple pot. You could make chopsticks anywhere by breaking wood, so we carried only one pot. So when we cooked and sat down together, it was really a poor situation. (laughter) There was nothing we didn't miss. That is a poor situation. A situation that knows how to miss things. What Jesus said about the hungry and thirsty being blessed is all true. When your stomach growls, there is nothing you don't miss in that poor situation. Even if it's just barley rice cake, it is more precious than a royal feast. There is nothing tasteless.

So when we started to eat, three young men sat down with one pot and began to eat. Even if one person wouldn't be satisfied, since we were sitting together, what would happen? Completion of Sacrifice
Everyone thinks of Reverend Moon of the Unification Church as a noble person sitting in a position of glory, right? That is a mistaken thought. When he is really tired, he sleeps in the car. So, he is grateful for being able to travel by car. He works hard. Even now, he is working hard. In the past, he was careful not to sleep while traveling in the car, but now the time spent in the car is his rest time. If he does not sleep in the car and takes a nap elsewhere, he is someone who repents upon waking. After taking a nap, he is a person who repents. Even now, when I go to factories, there are young boys and girls working, and just because I am tired does not mean I take a nap. If I feel sleepy, I sit and doze off... It is not because someone is watching.

Why is that? Because God does not rest for 24 hours. Has there ever been a time in the past 6,000 years when God decided to rest for even one hour? If there had been, was there ever a son or daughter who urged, "Father, please rest for just one hour?" There was not.

A parent who is on the path of life, which leads to death, and who seeks the connection of love with their children is not a parent who says they will sleep or rest. Living with such a God, I can sleep when I am tired for 24 hours, and I can rest at night, but when I think that God is working for me or for the Unification Church without resting, I realize that I owe a debt to God.
