The Korean people are well aware that everyone is hoping for unification. When considering the cause of the division between North and South, it may be said that the Korean War was the cause, but when we delve into the fundamental issues, we realize that it is due to the historical path that has prevented the world from becoming one.

Humanity and the world that are not unified
Even when it comes to individuals, we see that there are differing opinions and claims. Expanding the scope, even among one tribe, we find that the historical backgrounds and desired directions of hope differ. Given that the claims and positions are different, we observe corresponding relative phenomena or conflicting phenomena arising. Therefore, even if a certain ethnic group desires unification centered on a specific ethnicity, such unification is difficult to expect.

So far, there have been many sovereigns who have sought to unify the world’s nations, starting from individuals to their tribes or nations. However, we know that they have not found the path to unification through the natural environment.

When we look at the current world divided into the democratic world and the communist world, we see that these two worlds have different origins and different purposes. Since the starting point and purpose are different, the processes they go through must also be different. Therefore, we encounter conflicting phenomena. Some may hope for such a situation, while others oppose it, as we observe in our daily lives.

When considering these various issues, we ponder where we should begin to pursue unification. Attempting to address the resulting phenomena only repeats what has not been accomplished in historical times, so today we must seek solutions to this issue from a more fundamental perspective.

From this viewpoint, how are we as humans? If we were the basis and subject of unified oneness, it would be one thing, but when we observe humanity itself, we find that it is divided into two. Humans have bodies and minds. However, we discover that these bodies and minds are not completely unified.

From this perspective, we can say that there is a person of the heart and a person of the body. The body and mind should always pursue an objective purpose according to the conditions of the environment, yet we are well aware that they do not align with each other, meaning that the life of conscience and the life of reality do not correspond.

Where to establish the origin of unification
So where should we establish the origin and factors of unification that humans pursue? Even if there is a being that serves as a motivation and factor beyond ourselves, can we find a subject that can unify ourselves, which cannot be integrated? We know that there has not been such a subject in the historical process.

Even if there were a saint who established such a purpose, looking at the historical and realistic circumstances where the world or nations could not unify around that purpose, we realize that even if there is a subjective unifying factor, if we ourselves do not stand in a position aligned with that, it is extremely difficult to theorize and universalize this.

As we delve deeper, the question arises whether there is a God, that is, an absolute being. If there is an absolute being who created humans, should created humans stand in opposition to that absolute being or in compliance? When we consider this issue, if there is an absolute being, it must pursue an absolute purpose, and since humans, created by that being, are the only beings that can relate to that absolute being, they should pursue an absolute purpose as well. However, when we think about the fact that this is not currently the case, we arrive at a contradictory conclusion.

If humans are created by one absolute being, they should have a relationship where all environments, living conditions, and processes can be unified around one purpose. Yet when we discover that we are not in that position, we begin to question whether God truly exists.

Furthermore, when we clarify and analyze ourselves, we see that we possess two purposes, leading us to wonder if we are not beings created by one who pursues a single purpose, which brings the question of God's existence to the forefront.

So, in today’s world situation, where should we seek a solution or an ideological realm or a unified ideological world? It is neither the world nor any specific nation. The source from which we can pursue this is humanity. We must seek it among humans.

When we say 'human', there are both men and women. What are these men and women walking towards? They are walking through the stage of life, following historical directions. In this context, we are living our lives on the stage of reality, and we know that the direction of that life is diverse.

Some people go this way, while others go that way; some sit, while others stand; some come and some go. The forms of ascent and descent, and the directions of coming and going, change frequently depending on the environmental conditions.

However, if there is a God who governs, then the direction of that governance is absolute and cannot change. The direction of that governance must start from a unified fortune and be propelled toward the world of purpose based on harmonious and unified factors.

If such a God exists, then when we consider how we discover ourselves in relation to that God, we encounter fundamental issues centered around religion and life philosophy.

If God exists, that God must stand as an absolute subject before objective beings. A God alone cannot feel authority and satisfaction as a God. Joy and sorrow do not occur in isolation; they occur in a world related to relative conditions. Just as we seek joy beyond the place of sorrow based on relative relationships, the absolute being cannot find the conditions to rejoice as an absolute being in solitude.

So what is the objective being that can bring the greatest joy to that being? It is not any insignificant creature or animal among all things. The only being that can pursue objective value before the absolute subject is, upon consideration, humanity.

What kind of being must such a human be? They must be a relative absolute being that can stand before the absolute being. Therefore, they must stand in a position where the absolute being can rejoice. However, they do not wish to relate to that joy as something temporary. No one desires to be joyful today only to disappear tomorrow. If one has formed a connection in a joyful place, they wish to hold onto that in their hearts.

I am someone who enjoys fishing. When I fish in Cheongpyeong, I catch several big carp. I caught the biggest carp in Cheongpyeong, nearly 1 meter and 10 centimeters long. The thrill of catching it is truly exciting. (Laughter) I am now thinking of using Korea as a base to spread my line across the Pacific to catch America. I hope the line does not break; I hope the skill is sufficient. If you grab hold of it, it will not escape and will be caught...  
To catch a big carp, you cannot just rely on strength. If you do, either the carp's mouth will tear, or the line will break. It took me more than an hour to catch it because of how strong it was. A true filial son

Let’s say there is a filial son. This son is waiting to respond with "Yes" before his father gets up and says, "Hey, so-and-so!" He is a filial son with no faults. A filial son must absolutely obey his parents, right? To become a filial son, one must absolutely obey their parents’ words.

One day, the mother and father say, "So-and-so, you have worked hard, so we have something special prepared for you." "What is it?" "We want to give you the best clothes in the world, so we have saved every penny for the past 20 years. This is to repay your deep filial piety. Today, enjoy a nice suit, a gold ring, and a gold watch," and they give him several million won. Then the parents say, "You must never give these to anyone. Listen to your parents. You must never give them away." The filial son replies, "Yes, I will do that."

After putting on the clothes, he must have felt very good. He felt good, but he thought he shouldn’t just be happy by himself. Whether he is the eldest son or the youngest son doesn’t matter. He quietly thinks of his older brother and younger siblings. "I want to give it to my brother more than I want to wear it; I want to give it to my younger sibling." Such feelings arise. So, even though the parents said not to give it to anyone, he wanted to give it away, saying, "Oh, I don’t care." He gave the suit to his brother, the gold ring to his younger sibling, and shared everything without telling his parents.

However, after a while, the parents noticed that the filial son didn’t seem to be wearing the new clothes or having the watch or ring. So they said, "Hey, I gave you those clothes, and why don’t I see you wearing them these days?" The filial son replied, "Yes, that happened," while shedding tears. "Hey! Why are you like this?" "I’m actually sorry to you, Mom and Dad." "Why, why?" "I can’t say." Then he quietly left while shedding tears.

Now, if the son leaves without saying anything while the parents are asking, would that son be a filial son or a disobedient son? "He’s a disobedient son." Ma’am, is that son a filial son or a disobedient son? According to your answer, he would be a disobedient son. Later, when the parents feel bad and call him, they say, "I have boasted about you as a filial son in front of your siblings for ten years, but where is there such disobedience? You disobedient child!" The parents lament. When the parents say, "Did you think I wouldn’t know?" the filial son’s one word of opposition is more unjust than a hundred words of a disobedient child. Isn’t that right? Do you understand?

As the parents lament with their children gathered, the older brother and younger sibling are crying. The siblings think that it is ultimately because of them that their younger brother or older brother has become like this. So when the parents ask, "Hey! Why are you crying?" they all say, "We can’t answer," and leave.

For example, such a situation could happen. After all the children have left, only the naive youngest daughter remains. If someone is trying to take it from her and wants to have it, what would she do? If there is someone who wants to take it, where would she hide it? In a closet? In a safe?  
You watch movies, right? In a world where people tear apart safes filled with treasures, no matter how securely a safe is locked, what does it matter? Do you think they won’t break into the safe? They will take it away. So where can one feel safe? Where can one hide it and feel secure? If you research this, you will conclude that "I would like to hide it in a place that only I can see, where no one else can see." Isn’t that right? You want to hide it in a place that is visible only to you, known only to you, and unseen and unknown by the world.  
Then is there really a place in this world that is visible only to me, known only to me, and unseen and unknown by the world? When you look for it, the Bible says, "For where your treasure is, there your heart will be also" (Matthew 6:21). It is not that the heart is where the treasure is; rather, it is the other way around: where the treasure is, there the heart is. The heart follows the treasure. In today’s fallen world, such words are fitting. If the world had not fallen, the treasure would follow the heart.  
To fill the heart with treasure, can the heart be small? When asked, "How big is your heart?" can one say, "My heart is as small as the eye of a needle"? When asked, "How small is your heart?" can one say, "It is as small as a grain of sand"? Is your heart big or small? It is so big that it can hold a thousand or ten thousand worlds and still want to hold more. That is to make it one’s own possession. When it comes to greedy humans, God would want to lock Himself in the fence of His heart and lock it up tight. Don’t you feel the same? I do.

The person I love is someone I want to keep in my heart. They are in my heart. The current position in the racecourse
The path of struggle is the path of sacrifice

The Vatican might have become the headquarters of the Unification Church. If a few people had not opposed the Unification Church, it could have happened. From this perspective, we can see that history is not made by the whole but rather by whether one or two people do well or poorly. Therefore, you must clearly understand the current position of the Unification Church in this era. 
Do you understand why we need to pay attention to the members of established churches? “Yes.” 
Let’s make it possible for God to dwell in this land.
Right now, the biggest problem in the Republic of Korea is the religious issue. When viewed from the perspective of the Unification Church, Christianity is the most opposed. Isn’t that right? However, the day Christianity unites with us and is armed with unification ideology, Kim Il-sung of North Korea will not be a problem. We will bring Kim Il-sung from the spirit world. By 1972, Kim Il-sung will be 60 years old, and the Unification Church is preparing to confront that year.
Now in North Korea, they call Kim Il-sung “father,” right? “Yes.” In the Unification Church, we also call the teacher “father.” Isn’t that right? “Yes.” From this perspective, there are two fathers. (laughs) Without Kim Il-sung, restoration cannot happen. The relationship between Cain and Abel cannot be formed. Without external and internal confrontation, restoration cannot happen. From this viewpoint, we must unify North Korea. The Unification Church has established the International Victory Federation to prepare for this and has woven a net. Because we have gathered this entire nation into the Victory Federation externally, now a smooth interaction can permeate before this nation.
Do you understand? “Yes.” They are also trying to hand over the university campuses to us. It has already been proven that there is no ideology other than unification ideology. Do you understand? In that sense, our responsibility is important.
Everyone, do you want to visit the teacher’s hometown or not? “I want to go.” You should go, right? “Yes.” When you go to the hometown, the teacher will tell you all the stories from his childhood. The teacher will take you around and teach you what history is here and what history is there. Unification Church members who do not receive that teaching will have to toil for thousands of years in that land of North Korea. I won’t go into detail, but that time will come soon.
We must achieve unification through the northward advance. It is not about fighting with weapons, but rather fighting with words and theories. 
320   Current Position at the Racecourse
We must know our current position at the racecourse and, centered on God’s love, we must not lose to the established churches. Do you understand? “Yes.” Where will the God who has left the Korean established churches go? Have you thought about that? When you think about it, how pitiful God is. It has been nearly a hundred years of Christian history in Korea… This land, which has been blessed with things that are not in the history of the Bible, which was protected from invasion even during the Japanese occupation, is now trampled by Satan due to the Korean War… There is a reason for everything. It is true that God has left the established churches. Where will we place that God? Where should we place Him? The Unification Church must place Him, and then you yourselves must place Him.
Then have you placed God? When a teacher comes to your house to teach your children, don’t you go around buying food to treat him well? And when your son-in-law comes, don’t you borrow money to prepare for him? You do those things well, right? But have you ever done that to fulfill your father’s will? Have you ever placed Him?
Looking at the reality where denominations are fighting against each other, God cannot be there. We must place God, who has nowhere to go, in the Unification Church today. The one who came with a thousand-year dream, the one who must lay the foundation for eternal victory, you must become the embodiment of hope before Him and prepare yourself as a dutiful son or daughter. You must think about how to cultivate your heart and how to establish emotional connections. In light of these issues, can the Unification Church lose to the established churches? Can it lose to any past priests or nuns? We must place God closer than anyone else in history and serve Him better than we serve our own fathers. We must become a place where the king of the nation can come and rest, even if he has to leave his throne.
Whose house is such a house in this Korean land? Is it your house? Is your house such a place? Is it the house of those who claim to believe in the Unification Church? Is it a holy place where God can dwell, a global sanctuary that blooms with love and fragrance? Ladies here, when guests come to your house, don’t you treat them well? But is your house like that? Is it? When you are hungry, you eat; when you are cold, you wear clothes; when you are sad, you complain, but who knows the unjust circumstances of God, who is sorrowful and starving?
From this perspective, what should the men do? With the heart of welcoming the father into their homes, when they have money, they should buy something to offer to the father. Even if He is not physically present, they should kneel down and shed tears, saying, “I bring this offering of gratitude that I want to present to the father. Please accept this heart that offers this alone in place of the countless offerings that many ancestors have presented throughout history. Please forgive this nation for its wrongdoings and the wrongdoings of our ancestors.” They must be able to pray with weeping.
Moreover, they should take their sons by the hand and say, “Let’s go greet God.” They should want to share their sincerity and stories, but because the father is not physically present, they must hold their sons and weep.
Just like Abraham offered Isaac as a sacrifice, we must pray, “Is it not possible for You to accept me, my sons and daughters, and even myself as a sacrificial offering?” 
If they cannot create an environment where they can welcome the father with their wives, the couple should hold hands and pray, “Please accept us as offerings to resolve the grievances of the past. Accept us not as divided offerings but as offerings of familial victory.”
Now think about where God can be in this world. Where can that God, whom you call your father, be? Is it in your house? Think about your house. With all the complaints about food, living conditions, and everything else, if God were to enter your house, He would flee within two days, or even within one hour.
That is why, in this vast world, I must welcome God into the quiet room of my house. I believe that there is no one other than a burning son or daughter who wants to find and bring God, who would serve Him better than I could, who can comfort God in this era. Are you that person?
Let’s establish the tradition of welcoming. 
You must think about why the Unification Church has not been able to carry out the restoration providence centered around the globally renowned palace, and why Unification Church members have to endure such a path of suffering. You must realize that before I feel pity for myself, God feels pity. If there is someone who pours out all their sincerity to comfort God and who struggles on the path of spiritual hunger to praise God, that person will surely be with God.
will inherit God's love. Even if he lacks authority and has not prepared everything inside and out, if he has such feelings, God will still say that there is no place for me to be in this world, except for this house like Samak.

Therefore, if it is a house of someone who has such feelings, no matter how shabby that house may be, even if it is a thatched cottage, it will be my house, more than any palace in the world. The heartfelt meal served there, even if it is just a simple dish, can become a foundation for promising a happy future, and that is why God wants to rest there. This is how it happens. In this current position, you must become those who can absolutely welcome God, who has nowhere to go.

Then, where does God want to go through that family? He wants to go to the tribe through the family. Therefore, I must be at the forefront of paving the way for God to find the tribe. After finding the tribe, where will He go next? He will head towards the nation. Before God walks that path, I must first pave the way and accompany Him, and then I must pave the way to find the world and the nation, accompanying God. To love God in this way, even if I stand at the crossroads of insults, beatings, mockery, persecution, and death, I must have the heart that says, "Will my single-hearted devotion towards You ever change?" There is no other way.

Do you want to be happy just because you have met and received grace? You must not have such thoughts. You cannot just come and turn back. If you have come, you must take Him with you. You must take Him with you. Just as parents want to give the best to their beloved children first, and devoted children want to give good things to their elderly parents first, similarly, when it comes to serving God, if you go somewhere and stop by the market to buy good food and set it before God as a sign of devotion, that is not idolatry. If there is such a practical connection, how much would God be pleased? If a husband, wife, and children do that for God, then God can finally establish a connection in the human world centered around that family, a connection that can bring joy and hope. That family becomes the first family that God can relate to on this earth, and through the descendants of that family, history will turn around.

That is why the Unification Church teaches that salvation comes through serving. It is through service that we receive salvation. If there are men in suits for spring, summer, autumn, and winter, they must also serve their father. Since He does not have a physical body, when a season comes, if you collect your devotion and shed tears while offering it to the church with the heart of serving God, that is like the Ark of the Covenant. It should not be merely conceptual but should become a life that can be emotionally embodied and expressed.

Ultimately, this establishes a tradition that one must not be outdone in loving and serving God. Only by establishing such a tradition can it be good for his sons and daughters. You must create descendants in whom God can settle. Only then can you broaden the foundation for God to be present on this earth. This is not a simple matter.

Until now, I have never revealed my bare skin. Nowadays, I show a little because that time has passed. When I was in Hungnam prison working in a fertilizer factory, even in the hot summer months, I wore a belt. I did not expose my shins. These days, I wear short-sleeved shirts, but in the past, I really disliked such clothes. Because there remains a holy path that I must sweat through and offer to God, I did not want to show this body to anyone when it comes to serving God. So even when I slept alone, I did not stretch out my arms and legs. There is God above me. There is etiquette even in sleeping.

These days, the women of the Unification Church have very poor manners. I pretend not to see it, but a woman lies down in the daytime in the main room and snores loudly while taking a nap. Where in the world is there such a rude woman? God does not rest even at this time. When I think of that, it is wrong to sleep. God has been standing in a position where He cannot rest for 6,000 years, walking the path of restoration to determine your fate, and even now, He is protecting you to make a decision between life and death, so how can you sleep? How can you spread your arms and sleep just because it is time to sleep? Even if you sleep, you should pray while lying down. If you are really tired, then you can lie on your side. After sleeping like that, you have no responsibility. If you want to throw it away, you can throw it away, and if you don’t, that is fine. You must live like that.

God is someone who, when He sees something wrong wherever He goes, grieves and sheds tears in secret. God is now on the path to establishing tribes, nations, and states, so wherever you go, you must love God. You must understand that you cannot be a son or daughter living without that heart.

The current position of the Unification Church, standing at the racecourse to love God, is to serve God centered on the family and the tribe, and to go towards the nation and the world. Therefore, if you can bear the numerous trials and crosses that come, and if you can first walk the path of shedding tears, you will be able to receive even more of God's love. I hope you understand that such a path exists.

338   Season of Praise, Season of Victory
The most important year in the restoration course, 1971
You must understand that the year 1971 is the most important year in the restoration course. This year marks the fourth year of the second seven-year course, having completed three years. When we look at the history of the restoration providence, the second time has always been a problem. In the family of Adam, the second Abel was a problem, and in Noah's family, the second Ham was a problem. Even when we look at Adam, Noah, and Abraham, we know that the second Noah's time was centered around the family, through the connection of judgment. Furthermore, when we look at the Son of God, we understand that in the times of Adam, Jesus, and the Second Coming, the second son, Jesus, was the center of the division between good and evil.

From this perspective, the most important period in our seven-year course is the second seven-year course. You also know well that the year 1971 is the peak of the second seven-year course. Everything that happens this year is not by chance. Even when we look at the global situation, we see that this situation is not happening by chance. We are moving forward, preparing for the ultimate historical peak.

No one can guarantee which direction this world will flow through the crossroads it faces. From a providential perspective, no matter how difficult the environment may be, that difficult environment is essential for the providence, and it will inevitably lead to a path where the providence can be victorious. This view is natural for us who know the restoration providence.

In this context, when we look at September from our principled perspective, the number 9 in September, when viewed through three stages, is a number that can be expressed as three times three (3×3=9). After passing through September, we have now reached the time of the number 10. Therefore, the remaining three months can be seen as a new season that can replace the number 12 with the number 3, making it the most important season.

Autumn is the season of harvest as well as the season of praise.
339
When we look at the year, this season is the season of harvest. It is more a season of harvest than a season of fruition. Moreover, historically, the year 1971 should be regarded as the year of praise. When we consider the year 1971, the period after this October, which is the season of harvest, must also be seen as a season of praise.

When we look at all things, everything grows according to its own cycle throughout the year, aiming for a time of fruition. Whether the rewards of their efforts are realized or not depends on the harvest. We know that when we look at all things, the season of harvest is the most joyful season for those things that have borne good fruit, while for those that have not borne fruit, the season of harvest can be seen as a sad season. Therefore, we can understand that this season is also a time to determine victory and defeat centered around the harvest.

When we look at a grain, for that grain to bring about a completely victorious result, it must have a master who nurtures it and put in great effort. The value of that effort and the rewards of that effort are directly linked to the harvest. Also, no matter how much effort the master puts in, the conditions in which the grain grows, the quality of the soil, and the environmental conditions it faces become significant issues. It must stand at the point of victory after going through a year of internal and external struggles toward its purpose in order to bring about a glorious harvest.

From this perspective, when we look at all things that can be harvested, we must praise those that have borne fruit. To bring about such fruit, they must go through a process of struggle that no one knows and that no one can imagine. Knowing that it is a shining harvest resulting from worthwhile efforts, we must praise it.

340   Season of Praise, Season of Victory
We must become new seeds that possess vitality.
From this perspective, just as all things are, the historical providence must also be the same. When we look at the historical providence, what time is it now? It is a time that determines victory and defeat in human history, just like the season of harvest. There will be good groups, evil groups, groups that can win, and groups that can lose. There will also be groups that, even if they have won, must reaffirm their commitment from that position, groups that have already inherited the starting point, and groups that, no matter how much they have won, cannot inherit the path of a new beginning.

If we see it this way, even if we have achieved fruitful results in the season of harvest, that should not be the end. It must become a harvest that can remain as new seeds for a fresh start in the next year. If we fail to meet that standard, no matter how much we have harvested, we cannot help but remain at a lower level.

When we look at the historical providence... Today, we know that the democratic world and the communist world are divided. We know that these two worlds are fighting. Each side hopes to claim victory and unify the world according to their own assertions. However, even if they hope to achieve their own victory and globalize, the decision of victory and defeat will inevitably come through heavenly fortune during the harvest period of 6,000 years of human history.

Then, when we look at the ideological realm, which ideology can inherit the fruits of the harvest in human history? From our perspective, it must be religion. When we consider which religion it should be, it must be a religion that always contains the connection of life.

Life must be connected through love in an environment that can be unified. It is in such a foundation that the new will of heaven will begin through a place where life can be centered or where love based on life can be unified, aiming for heaven. When we think of this, you must feel once again how great the mission of our Unification Church is today. In this era, we are starting a new generation of life that no one else has. We have emerged with a heart that loves God more than anyone else. 

From this perspective, we must become a historical fruit, and among that fruit, we must become seeds that can be newly selected and planted in the spring world of new unity, sprouting new shoots. 

To become such seeds, what must we do? No matter how much we have brought forth the fruits of harvest, we must be able to overcome the harsh waves that come before us. What are those waves? Just as winter follows the autumn harvest, a cold, merciless, and pitiful environment that leaves no room for compassion will come crashing down. We must not become seeds that lose their lives in such an environment, but rather, we must become seeds that possess the power of life and can transform that environment into a realm of life. 

Without becoming such seeds, we cannot remain as seeds that can welcome a new spring season, nor can we fulfill our responsibility to welcome the glory of heaven in the second spring season. We must feel once again that our responsibility is profound.

We must have a new conviction and resolve, and even if we face trials, pains, or all the difficulties that seem insurmountable, we must have the power of life to push through. In other words, we must possess the autonomy that is not subject to any restrictions or dominion before anyone, and with our own authority of life, we must be able to root ourselves and remain with the strength of life. Without that power of life, we cannot be cultivated as the fruits of harvest that can remain in the new era.

Possess the autonomy and conviction to push through external environments.
From this perspective, today, there are about 3 billion people living in the world, and when we say that our small group of the Unification Church bears such a mission, it is certain that if there are forces of evil, all of those forces will concentrate their attacks on the Unification Church. The more numerous we are, the more the evil forces that can attack us will diminish; conversely, the fewer we are, the stronger the evil will become in proportion to our numbers.

Therefore, when such environments confront us, we must have the autonomy and conviction to push through those environments. 

Moreover, this October, which marks the first day of the month, is particularly significant from the perspective of our purpose. When we examine the spiritual content, the historical course until now has presented the path of indemnity through Abel. The historical era that sacrificed good to save Cain and forgive evil may very well be a turning point with the arrival of this October of 1971.

That is why, until now, there have been many rulers in the world who do not know God. Many people have been self-important, unaware of the heights of heaven, but I believe that the time will come when they will be brought low. Figures like Kim Il-sung in the North and Mao Zedong in China, as well as those in the democratic world who are self-important, will enter an era where they will be brought low.

Thus, we understand that the period from 1971 to 1974 is a historical transitional period, a providential time when the figures of historical problems will fade away. As those figures disappear and their sovereignty and nations become unstable, the foundation of providence centered on a single purpose will become more solidified, and we, who have pledged to represent the will of the nation, will see the arrival of a new morning light and must resolve anew.

Knowing that such a time is coming, we must unite internally. We must bond externally. No matter how difficult the external environment may be, our Unification group should not worry about that difficult environment but should resolve to have a unified heart before heaven and be horizontally bonded. When that bonded strength manifests as a power that surpasses the 3 billion people of humanity, the world will start a new course in the direction we desire, and each of us must start anew with that conviction and determination.

Now, we must realize that the time has come to prepare for the three-year course after passing through 1971, and we must feel the responsibility to resolve and pledge on this first day of October.

We must recognize that we are the fruit of history.
When we look at the harvest of autumn, even if the labor of the master has been great and the process has been difficult, if that harvest has been gathered in a way that brings joy to the master, how delighted will the master be when looking at that harvest? How much will he praise that harvest? This goes without saying.

From this perspective, today, our Unification group is a group that remains here as a result of the sacrifices made by many prophets and righteous ancestors throughout long historical eras. Knowing that the value of our existence today, as the fruit of that history, is infinite, each of you must learn to respect one another. When a single family member is properly planted in good soil, it can yield a hundredfold, a thousandfold, or ten thousandfold, creating a new foundation for the glory of heaven that can illuminate the world stage.

From this perspective, we must recognize how precious each family member is and respect them. If they have a path of tears, a path of suffering, and a path of overcoming, that path is the foundation where God can pour out His heart, where God's heart can be fully invested. If you share your hearts, your sincerity, and your compassion with that foundation and cooperate, God will boast about you before the world of evil. This will become an absolute condition to present a new front against the authority that evil has established until now. This is a matter we must think anew.

Therefore, the Unification group that has emerged as the fruit of harvest today must recognize that it has become a precious existence that can fulfill its own commitments and practice what it has sworn before heaven. We must learn to praise them. We must acknowledge their valuable contributions and present ourselves as a praised existence without shame before anyone in the historical course. We must have the confidence to stand before the 3 billion people of this era or before those who hold authority in any advanced nation. Furthermore, we must be able to present this tradition to our righteous descendants who will be born in the future. You must understand that this season, which allows us to reaffirm our own resolutions, is the season of harvest and the season of praise.
From this perspective, we must realize that not only we humans, not only the members of our Unification Church, but also countless spirits in the spiritual world have indeed been established and gathered as a group of unity as a historical harvest. When we refer to this group as the group of unity, it is not just the humanity of today, but also the countless spirits who have shed blood as sacrificial offerings on the altar of martyrdom throughout history. The good spirits are looking at us and asking us to resolve the collective sorrow. They will feel a joy greater than that of having found a day of victory for themselves. We must not forget that there are many good ancestors in the spiritual world.

Make October 1971 a month of praise
Therefore, we are not people living for a single era. We represent three eras. Above, we represent the spiritual world, and from a realistic standpoint centered on this land, we represent the world. Regarding the future, we represent our descendants, and we have the responsibility to uphold the traditions of these three eras. When we think about this, if I take a step forward here, the three eras will be liberated, and if I take a wrong step, the three eras will be buried forever in an unfortunate history that cannot be measured, along with the sorrow of the defeated. When considering this, we must feel how great the lament and sorrow of the good ancestors connected to us is, and we must recognize that this place is not the future or the past, but the present.

In this present moment, on this first day of October, you must make a new resolution. Here, welcoming a shining new morning, you must embrace new hopes and prepare to meet the new spring season of Eden that heaven desires, where new seeds can be sown before the world of freedom and the world of creative freedom, beyond the realm of sovereign nations. When we think about this, welcoming such a day is a historical wish, a standard that the current religion hopes for in the historical era, a standard of goodness that future descendants can hope for, and the foundation of future wishes that good ancestors will start from. When we realize that this place begins because of us, because of this moment today, we must feel that we cannot help but make a resolution with a new heart both inside and outside through our mind and body.

In this context, as you look back on the past in October, you should not let this October be a month where you envy any good days that have existed in the historical era. You must be able to boast that the days after this October are a better season than any joyful day in the past, and recognize that this is an important season that must be left before heaven. When you think about this, you should reflect on the past and critically reassess your current position, making this first day of October more meaningful than any day in the past or present, and turning the upcoming days into a season of praise that you experience for the first time in your life, a season of praise that our Unification Church experiences for the first time.

Become the embodiment of praise
No matter how much the will has come, you must become the embodiment that can accept that will. To become such an embodiment, you must have a heart that is deeply connected to heaven. How much do you love God, and how much will you reap as a valuable harvest centered on God's love in the future? Centered on yourself, you must become a seed with a worthwhile origin of life for the future, growing into a tree, transcending the history of lament, despair, and blood in the new spring garden, and in a new heaven where glory, victory, and praise are intertwined, you must be able to fully exert the power of your true nature. You must resolve to make October a month where branches stretch, leaves grow, and flowers bloom, bearing new fruits within the realm of heavenly glory, welcoming descendants of glory rather than descendants of lament, and embracing a new beginning with a different dimension and origin.

From this perspective, when we consider the remaining three months and the three years in the seven-year course, we must spend these three months meaningfully so that the remaining three years in the latter half of the seven-year course can also be meaningful. You must know that there is a mission today in our church that must be determined by heaven regarding significant issues in Asia from 1971 to 1974, and I hope that each of you can prepare with the faith and resolution to receive this harvest season, through the stimuli from the environment, and further deepen your inner commitment.

From October onwards, it will be a season of victory and praise, so you must praise this season while also praising the group of unity. Furthermore, when the conditions for praise become centered around yourself, and you can proudly declare that the embodiment of the Father's praise is here, then there is historical significance in welcoming this October.

If you become such individuals and gather here to commit to such responsibilities, if not only you but also the group of unity spread across the nation can unite as one, and if this united church can be gathered before the Father as a fruitful entity representing many organizations, then it will indeed be a foundation of victory that can remove the origin of sorrow that God has longed for on a national level. With this issue in mind, I have briefly spoken with the title “The Season of Praise, The Season of Victory,” hoping that you will embrace the upcoming three months and three years with even greater significance.

(We sing the song of unity together)
<Prayer> Father, may you come to your insufficient and unworthy children of unity with your promise, so that we can kick away our sorrows and raise the flag of liberation high, and may the day come soon when we can offer the authority of victory before you amidst the praises of all nations.

Father, as we start this first day of October granted by your grace, may October become a month that brings you glory.

May this year be gathered as the year you love, and may the second seven-year course be gathered as a period of your victory.

With the wishes we hope for, may you be with us for a long time, and may the historical resolution of sorrow be realized in a unified world with all people. I ask this again, and I pray all these things in the name of True Parents. Amen.
